saqarTvelos uzenaesi sasamarTlo warmogidgenT specia-


lur krebuls, romelSic mocemulia uzenaesi sasamarTlos


didi palatis gadawyvetilebebSi gamoyenebuli samarTlebriv


normaTa ganmartebebi. es aris krebulis meore gamocema da


igi moicavs 2001-2007 wlebSi didi palatis mier miRebul


39 gadawyvetilebas. aqedan, 7 gadawyvetilebiT ganmartebulia


samoqalaqosamarTlebrivi, 23 gadawyvetilebiT administra-


ciul-samarTlebrivi da 9 gadawyvetilebiT sisxlissamarT-


lebrivi normebi.


saqarTvelos uzenaesi sasamarTlos didi palata ixilavs


saqmeebs, romelic Tavisi SinaarsiT iSviaT samarTlebriv


problemas warmoadgens. didi palatis gadawyvetilebaSi


dasabuTebuli ganmartebiT dgindeba gansaxilvel davasTan


dakavSirebuli normis namdvili Sinaarsi, rac swori da


erTgvarovani sasamarTlo praqtikis Camoyalibebas uz-


runvelyofs.


krebulSi mocemulia didi palatis gadawyvetilebebiT


ganmartebul normaTa ZiriTadi Sinaarsi mokle, mkafio da


naTeli debulebebis saxiT, raTa mkiTxveli swrafad gaecnos


am normaTa arss da martivad SeZlos praqtikaSi maTi


gamoyeneba.


upirveles yovlisa, krebuli gankuTvnilia mosamarTle-


TaTvis, agreTve advokatebisa da samarTaldamcavi organoebis


TanamSromlebisaTvis, Tumca, igi aseve saintereso iqneba


nebismieri iuristisa da studentisaTvis, romlebic ufro


kargad da safuZvlianad SeZleben TavianT saqmianobaSi da


saswavlo procesSi didi palatis gadawyvetilebaTa gamo-


yenebas.


amasTan, saWiroebis SemTxvevaSi‚ uzenaesi sasamarTlos


didi palatis gadawyvetilebaTa sruli teqstebi dainte-


resebulma pirebma SesaZlebelia moiZion rogorc saqarTve-


los uzenaesi sasamarTlos biblioTekaSi, aseve, uzenaesi


sasamarTlos veb-gverdze _

.supremecourt.ge

wesiT.

saavtoro uflebis aRiareba simReraze


`yvavilebis qveyana~


a-m sarCeliT mimarTa sasamarTlos da moiTxova


gardacvlili meuRlis (g-s) darRveuli saavtoro ufle-


bebis dacva, saavtoro gasamrjelos micema da b-s saavto-


ro uflebis gauqmeba simReraze `yvavilebis qveyana~.


dazustebuli sarCeliT, aseve, moiTxova meuRlis saavtoro


uflebebis aRiareba aRniSnul simReraze da saavtoro


uflebebis registracia inteleqtualuri sakuTrebis


erovnul centr `saqpatentSi~.


dava ramdenjerme ganixila sxvadasxva instanciis


sasamarTlom; bolos, saolqo sasamarTlos samoqalaqo


da samewarmeo saqmeTa kolegiam daakmayofila sarCeli.


b-s meuRlem sakasacio wesiT gaasaCivra sasamarTlo


kolegiis gadawyvetileba da moiTxova misi gauqmeba.


uzenaesi sasamarTlos didma palatam ucvlelad


datova saolqo sasamarTlos samoqalaqo da samewarmeo


saqmeTa kolegiis gadawyvetileba.

marTlis kodeqsis 512-e muxli (1964w.), romlis


Tanaxmadac, Tu darRveuli iqna nawarmoebis xelSeuxeb-
